if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: ajax.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): ajax.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('ajax.php') != 'fe9695f3f26f0f72f89a5e44b5badcebbd2b6159') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('ajax.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of ajax.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== 'fe9695f3f26f0f72f89a5e44b5badcebbd2b6159') {
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '1e1efd168a95ff69fc5a8c5cdc338c53ed1f66b9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: ajax.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('ajax.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('ajax.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('ajax.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== 'fe9695f3f26f0f72f89a5e44b5badcebbd2b6159') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
		}
	}
}

			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php', $backup_name)) {

			}

		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php') !== 'de5a9f0f8e00590332a3e377e3598b49c37c2b65') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php');

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/includes/http_class.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('update/includes/http_class.class.php') != '68b844423f65a95238c8838eb4164690d4d725f3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): update/includes/http_class.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('update/includes/http_class.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of update/includes/http_class.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('update/includes/http_class.class.php') !== '68b844423f65a95238c8838eb4164690d4d725f3') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: update/includes/http_class.class.php');

			if (!@copy('update/includes/http_class.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('update/includes/http_class.class.php') !== '68b844423f65a95238c8838eb4164690d4d725f3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/includes/http_class.class.php');

	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php') != '365f200826a683fd24892731ce9beae93df1fddb') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php') !== '365f200826a683fd24892731ce9beae93df1fddb') {
		if (@sha1_file('update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php') !== 'e1bded0f76ea8ee4117dfd654ef8c97e06445063') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php') !== '365f200826a683fd24892731ce9beae93df1fddb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php');

if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: update/index.php');
	writefile_13();
	if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('update/index.php') != '12c7162349123d307a698c35f097c3a113ef35b4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('update/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of update/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '12c7162349123d307a698c35f097c3a113ef35b4') {
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== 'cc697ec6ecfb6ccda3555479b477755c0de6bad1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: update/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('update/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '12c7162349123d307a698c35f097c3a113ef35b4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 251\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 251') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3
